SET DEFINE OFF;
SET SCAN OFF;

drop sequence seq_products;
create sequence seq_products
    INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1
    MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999 NOCYCLE
    NOCACHE NOORDER;
    
DELETE FROM PRODUCTS WHERE PRODUCT_ID>=0;
